#!/usr/bin/python

import sys

# Remove duplicated lines from the produced lower-case version
# note that the input is sorted

if __name__ == '__main__':
	previous_line = ''
	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip()
		# emit current line if it is different from previous line
		if line != previous_line:
			print '%s' % (line)
		previous_line = line

#!/usr/bin/python
import sys

# mapper counts lines and words of its input 
    
if __name__ == '__main__':
	word_count = 0
	line_count = 0

	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip()
		line_count += 1
		word_count += len(line.split())

	print '%s\t%s' % (word_count, line_count)

-----

Task 4 code begin

Mapper:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python

import sys

# return all two-word sequences of each line in list format
def words_seq(line, n):
  line = line.split()
  seq = []
  for i in range(len(line)-n+1):
  	seq.append(line[i:i+n])
  return seq

if __name__ == '__main__':
	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip()
		seq = words_seq(line, 2)

		for two_words in seq:
			# emit every sequence and its count -- 1
			print '%s\t%s' % (' '.join(two_words), 1)
-----


Reducer:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python
import sys

# reducer does the count given two-word sequence
# note that the reducer input is sorted by key

if __name__ == '__main__':
	prev_seq = ''
	value_total = 0

	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip()
		seq, value = line.split('\t', 1)
		value = int(value)

		# check if current sequence is the same as the previous one
		# if yes, increment the value(count).
		# Otherwise, emit the previous pair and recount the new one
		if prev_seq == seq:
			value_total += value
		else:
			if prev_seq:
				print '%s\t%s' % (prev_seq, value_total)
			value_total = value
			prev_seq = seq

	# Don't forget the last pair
	if seq == prev_seq:
		print '%s\t%s' % (prev_seq, value_total)
-----

Commands:

#!/usr/bin/python

import sys

# mapper is the same as task_4's

def words_seq(line, n):
  line = line.split()
  seq = []
  for i in range(len(line)-n+1):
  	seq.append(line[i:i+n])
  return seq

if __name__ == '__main__':
	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip()
		seq = words_seq(line, 2)

		for two_words in seq:
			print '%s\t%s' % (' '.join(two_words), 1)
-----


Reducer:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python
import sys

# reducer is the same as task_5's
# reducer is also used as combiner
# as a combiner, it used as aggregating step to lessen keys that are passed to the reducer

if __name__ == '__main__':
	prev_seq = ''
	value_total = 0

	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip()
		seq, value = line.split('\t', 1)
		value = int(value)

		if prev_seq == seq:
			value_total += value
		else:
			if prev_seq:
				print '%s\t%s' % (prev_seq, value_total)
			value_total = value
			prev_seq = seq

	if seq == prev_seq:
		print '%s\t%s' % (prev_seq, value_total)
-----

Commands:

# Remove existent output directory if any
hdfs dfs -rm -r /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_5.out

# MapReduce
# add combiner
hadoop jar /opt/hadoop/hadoop-2.7.1/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-2.7.1.jar \
-input /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_2.out \
-output /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_5.out \
-mapper mapper4.py \
-combiner reducer4.py \
-reducer reducer4.py \
-file mapper4.py \
-file reducer4.py 


# Display
hdfs dfs -cat /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_5.out/part-00001 | head -20

Q: Is it faster with a combiner?
A: Yes, I took 11min to finish the job without combiner but 4min less with combiner.

Task 6 code begin

Mapper:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python

import sys
import heapq

# each mapper takes part of task_5 output and extracts top20 frequent sequences
# heapq provides an implementation of heaq sort algorithm

if __name__ == '__main__':
    heap_queue = []
    for line in sys.stdin:
        line = line.strip()
        seq, value = line.split('\t',1)
        value = int(value)

        # push the value item onto the heap
        heapq.heappush(heap_queue, (value, seq))
        if len(heap_queue) > 20:
        	# Pop and return the smallest item from the heap
            heapq.heappop(heap_queue)

    # emit every top20 pair
    for value,seq in heap_queue:
        print '%s\t%s'%(seq,value)

-----

Commands:

# Remove existent output directory if any
hdfs dfs -rm -r /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_6.out

# MapReduce
# set key to be everything up to the second tab (line end) in the line
# sort by the second key numerically in descending order 
# use only one reducer
hadoop jar /opt/hadoop/hadoop-2.7.1/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-2.7.1.jar \
-D mapreduce.job.output.key.comparator.class=org.apache.hadoop.mapred.lib.KeyFieldBasedComparator \
-D stream.num.map.output.key.fields=2 \
-D mapreduce.partition.keycomparator.options="-k2,2nr" \
-D mapreduce.job.reduces=1 \
-input  /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_5.out \
-output /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_6.out \
-mapper mapper6.py \
-file mapper6.py


# Display
# Extract top20 from merged top20 results
# see part-00001 as the final result
hdfs dfs -cat /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_6.out/part-00000 | head -20 > top_20.txt
hdfs dfs -copyFromLocal top_20.txt /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_6.out/part-00001
hdfs dfs -cat /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_6.out/part-00001

Task 7 code begin

Mapper:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python
import sys

# mapper reads each value in a line
if __name__ == '__main__':
	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip()
		row_id, values = line.split('\t')
		value_list = values.split()
		
		for column_id in range(len(value_list)):
			# emit each value with column_id and row_id
			print '%s\t%s\t%s' % (column_id, row_id, value_list[column_id])
-----


Reducer:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python
import sys

if __name__ == '__main__':
    row = []
    prev_row_id = '0'
    for line in sys.stdin:
    	line = line.strip()
    	# set row_id to be column_id and column_id to be row_id 
    	# to achieve matrix transposition
        row_id, column_id, value = line.split('\t')

        if row_id == prev_row_id:
            row.append(value)
        else:
            if prev_row_id:
            	# emit previous row and rebuild a new row
                print '%s\t%s'%(prev_row_id,' '.join(tuple(row)))
                row = []
                row.append(value)
        prev_row_id = row_id
    # Don't forget to emit last row
    print '%s\t%s'%(prev_row_id,' '.join(tuple(row)))
-----

Commands:

# Remove existent output directory if any
hdfs dfs -rm -r /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_7.out

# MapReduce
# set row_id and col_id as keys
# sort by row_id, and then col_id numerically
# use only one reducer
hadoop jar /opt/hadoop/hadoop-2.7.1/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-2.7.1.jar \
-D mapreduce.job.output.key.comparator.class=org.apache.hadoop.mapred.lib.KeyFieldBasedComparator \
-D stream.num.map.output.key.fields=2 \
-D mapreduce.partition.keycomparator.options="-k1,1n -k2,2n" \
-D mapreduce.job.reduces=1 \
-input /data/assignments/ex1/matrixLarge.txt \
-output /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_7.out \
-mapper mapper7.py \
-file mapper7.py \
-reducer reducer7.py \
-file reducer7.py

# Display

		tag = line[0]

		# check tag, then store every components into variables
		if tag == "mark":
			courseId = line[1]
			studentId = line [2]
			grade = line[3]
			# emit one "mark" record
			print '%s\t%s\t%s\t%s' % (studentId, tag, courseId, grade)
		else:
			if tag == "student":
				studentId = line[1]
				name = line[2] 
				# emit one "student" record
				print '%s\t%s\t%s' % (studentId, tag, name)
-----


Reducer:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python
import sys

# I define each line of output as a record

if __name__ == '__main__':
	record = ''
	prev_tag = ''
	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip().split('\t')
		
		# Check tag
		tag = line[1]
		if tag == 'student':
			# if the tag change from "mark" to "student", it means a new record starts
			if prev_tag == 'mark':
				print record
				record = ''
			record = line[2] + ' -->'
			prev_tag = tag
		# if tag is "mark", continue to add mark_pair at the tail of record
		if tag == 'mark':
			mark_pair = '(' + line[2] + ',' + line[3] + ')'
			record = " ".join((record, mark_pair))
			prev_tag = tag
	# don't forget to emit last record
	print record
-----

# MapReduce
# set studentId and tag as keys
# sort map output by studentId and then tag
# partitioner guarantees lines with the same studentId go to the same reducer
hadoop jar /opt/hadoop/hadoop-2.7.1/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-2.7.1.jar \
-D mapreduce.job.output.key.comparator.class=org.apache.hadoop.mapred.lib.KeyFieldBasedComparator \
-D stream.num.map.output.key.fields=2 \
-D num.key.fields.for.partition=1 \
-D mapreduce.partition.keycomparator.options="-k 1n -k 2r" \
-D mapreduce.partition.keypartitioner.options=-k1 \
-partitioner org.apache.hadoop.mapred.lib.KeyFieldBasedPartitioner \
-input /data/assignments/ex1/uniLarge.txt \
-output /user/s1469577/s1469577_task_8.out \

-file mapper8.py \

Task 9 code begin

Mapper:
-----
#!/usr/bin/python
import sys
import re

# mapper emits student name and his/her grade point average(gpa) 

if __name__ == '__main__':
	name = ''
	grade = 0
	gpa = 0
	for line in sys.stdin:
		line = line.strip().split()
		# check if the student takes more than 4 courses
		if len(line) > 6:
			gpa = 0
			grade = 0
			name = line[0]
			for i in range(2,len(line)):
				# use regular expression module to extract the mark of each course
				grade += int(re.findall(r"[\w']+", line[i])[-1])
			# calculate the gpa
			gpa = float(grade)/(len(line)-2)
			# emit name/gpa pair
			print "%s\t%s" % (name,str(round(gpa,2)))
-----
